to buy shares’.\r\n\r\nThe app ‘How to buy shares’ is extremely suitable for both the beginning and advanced investor, because you can learn everything about online trading in CFD shares. No previous knowledge of the stock exchange is required. With this app you learn how you can buy shares on the stock market with small amounts starting from £100. Trading with small amounts of money is also known as CFD trading. A Contract For Difference (CFD) is a contract between buyer and seller. This involves an agreement that the seller pays the difference between the opening price and the closing price. CFD is an investment instrument with leveraging which enables you as an investor to gain a financial advantage from both rising and falling share prices. With CFD you can buy more shares on the stock market than with traditional investment, thanks to leveraging.\r\n\r\nAfter following this course you can begin trading for example on the London stock market or on the currency exchange market. In short, this app ‘How to buy shares’ is wishing to start and wishing to learn about investing in the stock market. You learn in steps how CFD trading Works and what it involves. So you can invest in the share prices of, amongst others, easyJet, Vodafone, Apple or Facebook. You can also trade on the English index, the ftse100. \r\n\r\nWhilst using the app you will learn how to buy CFD shares.
